\begin{letter}{N}
\fmtLemma{n'}
\fmtCrossreference{\textnormal{see} na or ni}

\fmtLemma{n-}
\fmtPOS{pf}
\fmtSense{subject and object agreement prefix of the first person singular on verbs}

\fmtLemma{na}
\fmtCitation{(n' be\-fo\-re vo\-we\-ls)}
\fmtPOS{prep}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{with}
\fmtExampleRL{Aba\-nya\-la ba\-nywa\-na\-nga\-na ku\-sai na Ba\-ruu\-li.}
\fmtExampleEN{The Banyala relate well with the Baruuli.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{and (noun phrase conjunction)}
\fmtExampleRL{OSyli\-via n’o\-Ru\-th ba\-ka\-li ba\-ko\-li mu\-no.}
\fmtExampleEN{Sylvia and Ruth are very hard-working women.}
\fmtSubentry(c)
\fmtSense{even, also, too}
\fmtExampleRL{Obo\-na n’o\-nko\-ko yee\-na amai\-te oku\-naa\-ba.}
\fmtExampleEN{See, even the hen can have a dust bath.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-ba}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-naa\-ba}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{intr}/\fmtTrans{tr}
\fmtPFV{naa\-bi\-re}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{to bathe, to wash oneself}
\fmtExampleRL{Maa\-re oku\-naa\-ba. Ya\-ka\-la twa\-be oku mu\-ko\-lo.}
\fmtExampleEN{I have finished bathing. Come and we will go to the party.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{to wash (\eg hands)}
\fmtExampleRL{Naa\-ba amai\-so otoo\-le\-mu ebi\-ne\-ni.}
\fmtExampleEN{Wash the eyes and remove the eye discharge.}
\fmtSubentry(c)
\fmtSense{(of hen) to have a dust bath}
\fmtExampleRL{Obo\-na n’o\-nko\-ko yee\-na amai\-te oku\-naa\-ba.}
\fmtExampleEN{See, even the hen can have a dust bath.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-bya}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-naa\-bya}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{tr}
\fmtPFV{naa\-bi\-rye}
\fmtSense{to wash (ghee to remove milk residue)}
\fmtExampleRL{Na\-sa\-ngi\-re oNa\-ka\-laa\-lo nga aku\-naa\-bya ama\-gi\-ta gaa\-mwe.}
\fmtExampleEN{I came across a Hima woman washing her ghee.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-la}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-naa\-la}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{intr}
\fmtPFV{nai\-re}
\fmtSense{(of liquids) to spread, to flow, to flood}
\fmtExampleRL{Amai\-zi ga\-nai\-re omu ki\-sii\-ka kyo\-na\-kyo\-na.}
\fmtExampleEN{The water has spread all over the room.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-ni}
\fmtPOS{interrog}
\fmtSense{who}
\fmtExampleRL{Naa\-ni oyo aku\-nye\-ta?}
\fmtExampleEN{Who is that calling me?}

\fmtLemma{naa\-nuu\-ka}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-naa\-nuu\-ka}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{intr}
\fmtPFV{naa\-nuu\-ki\-re}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{(of food) to go bad, to get cover with slime, to spoil}
\fmtExampleRL{Eme\-re ega\-gi\-re ebbaa\-ku ebi\-ku\-naa\-nuu\-ka.}
\fmtExampleEN{Food that has gone bad usually has slime.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{to be elastic, to stretch}
\fmtExampleRL{Olu\-ko\-bba lu\-ni lu\-naa\-nuu\-ka mu\-no.}
\fmtExampleEN{This rubber strap can be elastic.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-nuu\-la}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-naa\-nuu\-la}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{intr}
\fmtPFV{naa\-nwi\-re}
\fmtSense{to stretch, to make bigger}
\fmtExampleRL{Omwa\-la waa\-mwe anaa\-nwi\-re olu\-go\-ye lwa\-nge.}
\fmtExampleEN{His girl has stretched my cloth.}

\fmtLemma{naa\-ti}
\fmtPOS{adv}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{until today, to date, up to now}
\fmtExampleRL{Naa\-ti nkya\-li mu\-guu\-da.}
\fmtExampleEN{Up to now I am still rich.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{even now}
\fmtExampleRL{Naa\-ti nkwa\-ba Ka\-mpa\-la.}
\fmtExampleEN{Even now I am going to Kampala.}

\fmtLemma{na\-baa\-na}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-baa\-na}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a}
\fmtSense{uterus}
\fmtExampleRL{Omwa\-na akuu\-ra mu na\-baa\-na.}
\fmtExampleEN{A child grows in the uterus.}

\fmtLemma{na\-ba\-lii\-sya}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-ba\-lii\-sya}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/10}
\fmtSense{omasum}
\fmtExampleRL{Ona\-ba\-lii\-sya abba mu nda ya ki\-so\-lo ng’ai\-sa\-na empa\-pu\-la.}
\fmtExampleEN{An omasum is found in the stomach of an animal and looks like papers.}

\fmtLemma{Na\-ba\-yi\-nda}
\fmtCitation{(o)Na\-ba\-yi\-nda}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/2}
\fmtSense{female member of one of the clans of the Monkey totem}

\fmtLemma{na\-bbi}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-bbi}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/2}
\fmtSense{prophet}
\fmtExampleRL{Ebi\-ga\-mbo bya na\-bbi Isaa\-ya byai\-ki\-rii\-re.}
\fmtExampleEN{The words of prophet Isaiah came to true.}

\fmtLemma{na\-bbo\-ne\-ra}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-bbo\-ne\-ra}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/10}
\fmtSense{type of shrub with straight stems used to make doors and fences}

\fmtLemma{na\-bbwo\-ri}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-bbwo\-ri}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a}
\fmtSense{mould on fermented millet flour}

\fmtLemma{na\-bu\-ge\-re}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-bu\-ge\-re}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a}
\fmtSense{tinea pedis, athlete's foot}
\fmtExampleRL{Ona\-bu\-ge\-re asii\-ya mu\-no.}
\fmtExampleEN{The athlete's foot infection is very itchy.}

\fmtLemma{Na\-bu\-zaa\-na}
\fmtDialect{Lu\-nyala}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-bu\-zaa\-na}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a}
\fmtSense{type of god, female spirit believed to come from Bu\-nyoro}
\fmtExampleRL{ONa\-bu\-zaa\-na ni\-ye mba\-ndwa aga\-ba olu\-bya\-lo.}
\fmtExampleEN{Nabuzaana is a spirit that blesses people with birth.}

\fmtLemma{na\-da\-la}
\fmtPOS{adv}
\fmtSense{especially, mainly, mostly, chiefly, principally, largely}
\fmtExampleRL{Omu\-sa\-ngo gwa\-ku\-wei\-re na\-da\-la si\-nga wa\-kwa\-ta\-gai\-ne n’o\-mu\-la\-mu\-li.}
\fmtExampleEN{The case would have ended especially if you had cooperated with judge.}

\fmtLemma{na\-fu\-wa}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-na\-fu\-wa}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{intr}
\fmtPFV{na\-fu\-wi\-re}
\fmtSense{to become weak, to weaken}
\fmtExampleRL{Onte wa\-nge ana\-fu\-wi\-re.}
\fmtExampleEN{My cow has become weak.}

\fmtLemma{na\-ga}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-na\-ga}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{tr}
\fmtPFV{na\-gi\-re}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{to drop, to fall}
\fmtExampleRL{Enju\-ra eta\-ndi\-ki\-re oku\-na\-ga ama\-to\-ndo.}
\fmtExampleEN{The rain has started falling.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{to throw away, to toss away, to hurl}
\fmtExampleRL{Ei\-saa\-nii\-ko li\-ni li\-na\-ge omu lu\-su\-ku.}
\fmtExampleEN{Throw away the used banana leaves in the banana plantation.}
\fmtSubentry(c)
\fmtSense{to lose, to fail to keep}
\fmtExampleRL{Ana\-gi\-re empii\-ya zaa\-mwe z’a\-bai\-re akwi\-rya\-yo omu bba\-nka.}
\fmtExampleEN{She has lost her money which she was supposed to repay as a loan in the bank.}
\fmtSubentry(d)
\fmtSense{to abandon, to leave behind, to forget, to dump, to neglect}
\fmtExampleRL{Omu\-ka\-li ya\-na\-gi\-re omwa\-na waa\-mwe n’a\-ya\-ba.}
\fmtExampleEN{The woman abandoned her child and left.}
\fmtSubentry(e)
\fmtSense{(of wind) to uproot, to blow away}
\fmtExampleRL{Ompu\-ngo ana\-gi\-re emi\-saa\-le.}
\fmtExampleEN{The wind has uprooted the trees.}
\fmtSubentry(f)
\fmtSense{to lay (eggs), to produce (larvae)}
\fmtExampleRL{Onko\-ko ya\-ta\-ndi\-ki\-re oku\-na\-ga ama\-wu\-li.}
\fmtExampleEN{The hen started laying eggs.}
\fmtSubentry(g)
\fmtFixedexpression{na\-ga (a)ka\-sa\-ya}
\fmtSense{(idiom, lit.\,to loose the jaw) to die, pass on, pass away}
\fmtExampleRL{Ba\-mbi omu\-kai\-re ana\-gi\-re aka\-sa\-ya.}
\fmtExampleEN{Oh dear, the old woman has passed on. (lit.\,The old woman has lost the jaw.)}

\fmtLemma{na\-ga\-nso\-byo}
\fmtCitation{(o)na\-ga\-nso\-byo}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/10}
\fmtSense{horn worm, hawk moth (\textit{Agrius convolvuli})}
\fmtExampleRL{Ona\-ga\-nso\-byo atu\-ma\-lii\-re ebi\-yaa\-ta.}
\fmtExampleEN{The hawk moth has destroyed all our sweet potatoes.}

\fmtLemma{na\-gi\-ri\-za}
\fmtCitation{(oku)\-na\-gi\-ri\-za}
\fmtPOS{v}%
\fmtTrans{tr}
\fmtPFV{na\-gi\-rii\-ze}
\fmtSense{to neglect, to fail to look after}
\fmtExampleRL{Otaa\-ta ya\-na\-gi\-ri\-ze abaa\-na baa\-mwe boo\-na ndoo\-wo ya\-so\-me\-re.}
\fmtExampleEN{The father neglected all his children, none went to school.}

\fmtLemma{na\-gu\-ni}
\fmtPOS{adv}
\fmtSense{up to now}
\fmtExampleRL{Na\-gu\-ni ti\-mu\-bo\-naa\-nga\-ku.}
\fmtExampleEN{Up to now I have never seen him.}

\fmtLemma{na\-ki}
\fmtCitation{\textnormal{(e.g.}\,mu\-na\-ki, ba\-na\-ki, ka\-na\-ki\textnormal{)}}
\fmtPOS{adj}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{weak}
\fmtExampleRL{Ti\-ki\-kwe\-wuu\-nyi\-sya no maa\-wo yaa\-li mu\-na\-ki.}
\fmtExampleEN{No wonder, even your mother was a weakling.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{lazy}
\fmtExampleRL{Nywe\-te mu\-li ba\-na\-ki mu\-no ti\-mu\-so\-bo\-la na\-ku\-lo\-ngoo\-sa we mu\-su\-la!}
\fmtExampleEN{You are very lazy people, you cannot even clean where you stay!}

\fmtLemma{na\-ku}%
\fmtOne{1}
\fmtCitation{(e)na\-ku}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{9/10}
\fmtSense{day}

\fmtTrans{tr}
\fmtPFV{nywi\-si\-rye}
\fmtSense{to take (cattle) to a drinking pond}
\fmtExampleRL{Nkwa\-ba ku\-nywi\-sya nte.}
\fmtExampleEN{I am taking the cattle to a watering pond.}

\fmtLemma{nywi\-syo}
\fmtCitation{(e)nywi\-syo}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{9/10}
\fmtSense{filter}
\fmtExampleRL{Olu\-se\-ke lwa ma\-lwa lu\-bbaa\-ku enywi\-syo.}
\fmtExampleEN{The local straw used to drink beer has a filter.}

\fmtLemma{nzai}
\fmtCitation{(e)nzai}
\fmtPOS{adv}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{outside}
\fmtExampleRL{Awu\-lu\-ki\-re nzai.}
\fmtExampleEN{She has gone outside.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{abroad, overseas}
\fmtExampleRL{Aku\-bi\-nga ku bya\-ku\-fu\-na paa\-si\-poo\-ta kwa\-ba nzai.}
\fmtExampleEN{Bukenya went abroad.}
\fmtSubentry(c)
\fmtSense{out of wedlock}
\fmtExampleRL{OMa\-gu\-zi aboi\-ne ku\-bba ba\-mu\-byai\-re nzai.}
\fmtExampleEN{It is a pity that Maguzi was born out of wedlock.}

\fmtSense{type of fish}

\fmtLemma{nzi\-ngo}

\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{9}

\fmtLemma{nzi\-nzi\-mi\-ya}

\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{9/10}

\fmtExampleRL{Aba\-si\-raa\-mu aba irai ba\-ko\-le\-sya\-nga nzi\-nzi\-mi\-ya oku\-fu\-na wu\-zu.}
\fmtExampleEN{In the past Muslims used kettles for ablution.}

\fmtLemma{nzi\-ra}

\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{9/10}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{road, way, path, street}
\fmtExampleRL{Na\-ya\-gii\-rye eki\-so ki\-ni oku nzi\-ra.}
\fmtExampleEN{I found this machete beside the road.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtFixedexpression{sa\-la (e)nzi\-ra}
\fmtSense{to cross, to cross over}
\fmtExampleRL{Asaa\-re enzi\-ra n’ai\-ra oku ki\-na\-nzi\-ra ki\-di.}
\fmtExampleEN{He has crossed the road and gone to the other side.}

\fmtLemma{nzo\-ka}
\fmtCitation{(o)nzo\-ka}
\fmtPOS{n}%
\fmtNC{1a/10}
\fmtSubentry(a)
\fmtSense{generic term for all intestinal warms}
\fmtExampleRL{Ombu\-li wa\-nge mu\-lwai\-re wa nzo\-ka.}
\fmtExampleEN{My goat has tapeworms.}
\fmtSubentry(b)
\fmtSense{abdominal pain, stomach ache}
\fmtExampleRL{Ndi mu\-lwai\-re wa nzo\-ka.}
\fmtExampleEN{I am suffering from abdominal pain.}
\fmtSubentry(c)
\fmtFixedexpression{sa\-la (e)nzo\-ka}
\fmtSense{to have sexual intercourse after the birth of a baby}
\fmtExampleRL{Aba\-fu\-mbo ba\-sa\-la enzo\-ka olu\-zwa\-nyu\-ma lwa ki\-see\-ra eki\-ma\-la.}
\fmtExampleEN{The couple has sex after a sufficient period after the birth of a child.}
